--- Commit Message ---
LU-10181 mdt: read on open for DoM files

Read file data upon open and return it in reply. That works
only for file with Data-on-MDT layout and no OST components
initialized. There are three possible cases may occur:
1) file data fits in already allocated reply buffer (~9K)
   and is returned in that buffer in OPEN reply.
2) File fits in the maximum reply buffer (128K) and reply is
   returned with larger size to the client causing resend
   with re-allocated buffer.
3) File doesn't fit in reply buffer but its tail fills page
   partially then that tail is returned. This can be useful
   for an append case

Test-Parameters: mdssizegb=20 testlist=sanity-dom,dom-performance,racer

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2018-02-01 16:46:04.000000000) ---
Patch Set 31: Code-Review-1

(6 comments)

For this to land, I think at a minimum there needs to be a client-side /proc tunable to control whether any pre-read is done, and how much should be read. I can easily imagine that we want to read up to 32KB on open, since this is how much space we have for large layout xattrs, and beyond that we should do a separate bulk read. A later patch could add runtime checks to stop the MDS pre-read operation if some thread is not using the data. 

Ideally, we should also be able to share the client reply buffer space between the LOV xattr and the pre-read buffer, rather than having to allocate a large reply space for both but not using one or the other.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2018-02-01 19:00:44.000000000) ---
Patch Set 32:

For auto-detection, we could do something similar to readahead or stay ahead - to track the number of files opened by some process, then how many of them are being read. If a large fraction of the files are read, then continue prereading, if a small fraction are read then stop preread. Alternately, only preread if a sequence of files is being opened and read. 

Unless we have data stored directly in the inode, the reads are not totally free, both because of extra IO on the MDS, but also because of increased network traffic. 

That said, I think with a tunable for the preread size I think it is enough for now, and other issues are more important to fix, such as automatically handling the MDT component size if some MDT has max size = 0, or is running out of space.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2018-02-01 19:03:03.000000000) ---
